 28: uses('magic_db', 'object');
 29: /**
 30:  * The test class for the MagicDb classA
 31:  *
 32:  * @package     cake.tests
 33:  * @subpackage  cake.tests.cases.libs
 34:  */
 35: class MagicDbTest extends UnitTestCase {
 36: /**
 37:  * The MagicDb instance to be tested
 38:  *
 39:  * @var object
 40:  * @access public
 41:  */
 42:     var $Db = null;
 43: 
 44: /**
 45:  * Sets up a MagicDb class instance for testing
 46:  *
 47:  * @access public
 48:  */
 49:     function setUp() {
 50:         $this->Db =& new MagicDb();
 51:     }
 52: 
 53: /**
 54:  * MagicDb::analyze should properly detect the file type and output additional info as requested.
 55:  *
 56:  * @access public
 57:  */
 58:     function testAnalyze() {
 59:         $r = $this->Db->read(MagicDbTestData::get('magic.db'));
 60:         $this->assertTrue($r === true);
 61: 
 62:         $r = $this->Db->analyze(array());
 63:         $this->assertTrue($r === false);
 64: 
 65:         $r = $this->Db->analyze(WWW_ROOT.'img'.DS.'cake.icon.gif');
 66:         // TODO: Check several serialized file samples for accurate detection
 67:     }
 68: 
 69: /**
 70:  * MagicDb::read should properly read MagicDb databases from .php-/.db-files and plain data arguments passed in and return false if the file wasn't found or
 71:  * if the readed data did not validate.
 72:  *
 73:  * @access public
 74:  */
 75:     function testRead() {
 76:         $this->Db->db = array();
 77: 
 78:         $r = $this->Db->read(true);
 79:         $this->assertTrue($r === false);
 80:         $r = $this->Db->read(5);
 81:         $this->assertTrue($r === false);
 82: 
 83:         $this->Db->db = array('a');
 84:         $r = $this->Db->read(array('foo' => 'bar'));
 85:         $this->assertTrue($r === false);
 86:         $this->assertTrue($this->Db->db === array('a'));
 87: 
 88:         $magicDb = array('header' => array(), 'database' => array());
 89:         $r = $this->Db->read($magicDb);
 90:         $this->assertTrue($r === true);
 91:         $this->assertTrue($this->Db->db === $magicDb);
 92: 
 93:         // @TODO: Test parsing an actual magic.db file
 94: 
 95:         $r = $this->Db->read('does-not-exist.db');
 96:         $this->assertTrue($r === false);
 97:         $this->assertTrue($this->Db->db === $magicDb);
 98: 
 99:         if (file_exists(VENDORS.'magic.php')) {
100:             $r = $this->Db->read(VENDORS.'magic.php');
101:             $this->assertTrue($r === true);
102:             $this->assertTrue($this->Db->db === array('header' => array(), 'database' => array()));
103:         }
104: 
105:         $r = $this->Db->read(MagicDbTestData::get('magic.snippet.db'));
106:         $this->assertTrue($r === true);
107:     }
108: 
109: /**
110:  * MagicDb::toArray should either return the MagicDb::db property, or the parsed array data if a magic.db dump is passed in as the first argument
111:  *
112:  * @access public
113:  */
114:     function testToArray() {
115:         $this->Db->db = array();
116: 
117:         $r = $this->Db->toArray();
118:         $this->assertTrue($r === array());
119:         $this->Db->db = array('foo' => 'bar');
120:         $r = $this->Db->toArray();
121:         $this->assertTrue($r === array('foo' => 'bar'));
122: 
123:         $r = $this->Db->toArray(array('yeah'));
124:         $this->assertTrue($r === array('yeah'));
125: 
126:         $r = $this->Db->toArray('foo');
127:         $this->assertTrue($r === array());
128: 
129:         $r = $this->Db->toArray(MagicDbTestData::get('magic.snippet.db'));
130:         $this->assertTrue($r === MagicDbTestData::get('magic.snippet.db.result'));
131:     }
132: 
133: /**
134:  * The MagicDb::validates function should return if the array passed to it or the local db property contains a valid MagicDb record set
135:  *
136:  * @access public
137:  */
138:     function testValidates() {
139:         $r = $this->Db->validates(array());
140:         $this->assertTrue($r === false);
141: 
142:         $r = $this->Db->validates(array('header' => true, 'database' => true));
143:         $this->assertTrue($r === false);
144:         $magicDb = array('header' => array(), 'database' => array());
145:         $r = $this->Db->validates($magicDb);
146:         $this->assertTrue($r === true);
147: 
148:         $this->Db->db = array();
149:         $r = $this->Db->validates();
150:         $this->assertTrue($r === false);
151: 
152:         $this->Db->db = $magicDb;
153:         $r = $this->Db->validates();
154:         $this->assertTrue($r === true);
155:     }
156: }
157: 
158: /**
159:  * Test data holding object for MagicDb tests
160:  *
161:  * @package     cake.tests
162:  * @subpackage  cake.tests.cases.libs
163:  */
164:

178: /**
179:  * Returns the test data for a given key
180:  *
181:  * @param string $key
182:  * @access public
183:  **/
184:     function get($key) {
185:         static $data = array();
186: 
187:         if (empty($data)) {
188:             $vars = get_class_vars(__CLASS__);
189:             foreach ($vars['data'] as $k => $v) {
190:                 $data[$k] = base64_decode($v);
191:                 if (preg_match('/^[ais]:[0-9]+/', $data[$k])) {
192:                     $data[$k] = unserialize($data[$k]);
193:                 }
194:             }
195:         }
196: 
197:         if (!isset($data[$key])) {
198:             return false;
199:         }
200:         return $data[$key];
201:     }
202: }
